#Create Insert Queries
#Materialization of FRs - Query1a:(RUN QUERY 6 BELOW TO MATERIALIZE THE NON-MATERIALIZED RELATIONS)

PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #0
$subject ^sealitFR:born_at_division_E21_Person2E53_Place ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/division_of_birth_of_E53_Place2E21_Person> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/E21_Person

}
#}#GRAPH
}}
###end

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #2
$subject a sealit:Ship .?value a crm:E21_Person .{$subject ((sealit:voyages|^sealit:voyage_of)/crm:P14_carried_out_by) ?value . ?value (sealit:has_profession|(sealit:had_provided/crm:P02i_is_range_of/crm:P.1a_in_the_role_of)) ?role .FILTER REGEX(STR(?role), "capitano", "i")} UNION {$subject (sealit:voyages/sealit:navigated_by_captain) ?value . }

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/had_captain_Ship2E21_Person> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/E21_Person

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #131
$subject a crm:E31_Document . $subject crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/doc%20types/source%20identity> .$subject crm:P46i_forms_part_of ?collection .?collection a crm:E78_Collection .$subject crm:P102_has_title ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/forms_part_of_collection_Source2Title> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/Title

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>

PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #146
?course a sealit:Course . ?course crm:P1_is_identified_by ?title .?title a crm:E35_Title .BIND (?course as $subject)BIND (?title as $value)

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/has_title_Course2Title> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/Title

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #164
$subject ^sealitFR:has_owner_organisation_with_headquarters_location_Ship2E40_Legal_Body ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/is_the_owner_organization_for_E40_Legal_Body2Ship> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#Ship

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #181
$subject a sealit:Ship .$subject (sealit:voyages|^sealit:voyage_of) ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/related_to_voyage_Ship2Voyage> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#Voyage

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #228
$subject a crm:E21_Person .$subject sealit:had_provided ?empl . ?empl crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/service%20types/company> .?empl crm:P4_has_time-span/crm:P82a_begin_of_the_begin ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/provided_service_starting_on_E21_Person2date> as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#date

BIND( year(xsd:dateTime((?value))) as ?year )

FILTER( BOUND(?ok) && ?ok )

}
#}#GRAPH

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND (<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/has_days_at_sea_Voyage2decimal> as ?predicate)

#Materialization of inversed FRs - Query1b:(RUN QUERY 6 BELOW TO MATERIALIZE THE NON-MATERIALIZED RELATIONS)

PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #2
<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/had_captain_Ship2E21_Person> owl:inverseOf ?iFR .

$subject ^<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/had_captain_Ship2E21_Person> ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

#Confirm ?iFR:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/was_captain_at_E21_Person2Ship

Bind (?iFR as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#Ship

}
#}#GRAPH
}}

PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> { $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM } }
WHERE {
SELECT $subjectM ?predicate ?valueM WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
{ #165
<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/provided_for_employment_at_ship_Crew_Payment2Ship> owl:inverseOf ?iFR .

$subject ^<http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/provided_for_employment_at_ship_Crew_Payment2Ship> ?value .

OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

OPTIONAL {$valueMaster owl:sameAs ?value}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

BIND( IF(BOUND($valueMaster), $valueMaster, ?value) as ?valueM )

#Confirm ?iFR:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/was_provided_employment_for_payment_Ship2Crew_Payment

Bind (?iFR as ?predicate)

#Range:http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#Crew_Payment

}
#}#GRAPH
}}
###end

#Materialization Query2 (correlate subjects of specific types with Records/Documents && Materialize Record FC AT THE SAME TIME):
#Note: no need to look for the masters because the materialization graph contains only the master IDs

PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT
{ GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> {
$subjectM ?relation ?record .
?record ?inverseRelation $subjectM .
?record a sealitFC:Record .
}}
WHERE {
#GRAPH ?g {
?record a crm:E73_Information_Object .
?record crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/doc%20types/record%20information> .
?record crm:P67_refers_to ?doc . ?doc a crm:E31_Document .
?template crm:P67_refers_to ?record .
?template crm:P67_refers_to $subject .
$subject a ?sType .
OPTIONAL {$subjectMaster owl:sameAs $subject}

BIND( IF(BOUND($subjectMaster), $subjectMaster, $subject) as $subjectM )

#}
VALUES (?sType ?relation ?inverseRelation) {
( sealit:Ship sealitFR:Ship2Record sealitFR:Record2Ship )
( sealit:Voyage sealitFR:Voyage2Record sealitFR:Record2Voyage )
( crm:E21_Person sealitFR:Person2Record sealitFR:Record2Person )
( crm:E40_Legal_Body sealitFR:Legal_Body2Record sealitFR:Record2Legal_Body )
( crm:E53_Place sealitFR:Place2Record sealitFR:Record2Place )
( sealit:Ship_Crew_Employment sealitFR:Ship_Crew_Employment2Record sealitFR:Record2Ship_Crew_Employment )
( sealit:Crew_Payment sealitFR:Crew_Payment2Record sealitFR:Record2Crew_Payment )
}}
###end

#Materialization Query3 (the generic relation "related to" among FCs with more than one FRs):
#Note:the generic "related to" gets instantiated when more than 1 relations exist. Avoid to name other relations as the generic "related to"

PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization_related_to> {?s ?relation ?o} }
WHERE {
{ SELECT DISTINCT ?s ?relation ?o {
{ SELECT DISTINCT ?sType ?oType (COUNT(DISTINCT ?p) as ?c) {
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> {?s ?p ?o }
?s a ?sType .
?o a ?oType .
VALUES ?oType {sealit:Ship sealit:Voyage crm:E21_Person sealit:Crew_Payment crm:E53_Place crm:E40_Legal_Body sealit:Course}
} GROUP BY ?sType ?oType }
FILTER (?c > 1)
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> {?s ?p ?o }
?s a ?sType .
?o a ?oType .
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR> {
VALUES ?relationLabel { "related to"@en }
?relation rdfs:label ?relationLabel; rso:hasDomain ?sType; rso:hasRange ?oType .
}
}}}
###end

#Materialization Query4a (sealitFC:Title):
#Helps SemanticSearch to find a resource-URI by its rdfs:label
PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

INSERT {GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/titles> { ?o rdf:type sealitFC:Title } }
WHERE {
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materialization> {?s ?FR ?o }
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR> {
?FR rso:hasRange sealitFC:Title .
}
}
###end

}

INSERT #NEW RDF TYPE
{
GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materializationTemplate> {
?subject rdf:type ?type .
?type rdfs:label ?type_label .}
}
WHERE {
VALUES (?type ?type_label ) {
(rso:Template "Template type" )
}
?template a crm:E73_Information_Object .
#?template (crm:P1_is_identified_by/crm:P2_has_type) <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/id%20types/record%20id> .
MINUS {?template crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/doc%20types/record%20information> }
?template crm:P2_has_type ?subject .
}
###end

#Materialization Query6 (rso:Template):

PREFIX rso: <http://www.researchspace.org/ontology/>
PREFIX crm: <http://www.cidoc-crm.org/cidoc-crm/>
PREFIX xsd: <http://www.w3.org/2001/XMLSchema#>
PREFIX rdf: <http://www.w3.org/1999/02/22-rdf-syntax-ns#>
PREFIX rdfs: <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#>
PREFIX owl: <http://www.w3.org/2002/07/owl#>
PREFIX skos: <http://www.w3.org/2004/02/skos/core#>
PREFIX sealit: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/sealit#>
PREFIX sealitFC: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FC/>
PREFIX sealitFR: <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FR/>

#SELECT $subject ?relation ?recordType
INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materializationTemplateInstances> {$subject ?relation ?recordType.} }
WHERE { #1
VALUES (?sType ?relation) {
( sealit:Ship sealitFR:Ship2Template )
#( sealit:Voyage sealitFR:Voyage2Template )
#( crm:E21_Person sealitFR:Person2Template )
#( crm:E40_Legal_Body sealitFR:Legal_Body2Template )
#( crm:E53_Place sealitFR:Place2Template )
##( sealit:Ship_Crew_Employment sealitFR:Ship_Crew_Employment2Template )
#( sealit:Crew_Payment sealitFR:Crew_Payment2Template )
#( sealit:Course sealitFR:Course2Template )
}
$subjectX a ?sType .
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by) $subjectX .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/(sealit:voyages|^sealit:voyage_of) $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Voyage .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/sealit:gave_service_for $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Crew_Payment .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/sealit:had_provided $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Ship_Crew_Employment .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/^(crm:P9_consists_of/sealit:had_student) $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Course .}
FILTER ( ?recordType != <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/template> )
OPTIONAL { $subjectM owl:sameAs $subjectX . $subjectM crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/type/master>. }
BIND (IF(BOUND($subjectM), $subjectM, $subjectX) AS $subject)
}
#LIMIT 10 #used with select for debugging
###end

INSERT { GRAPH <http://www.sealit.gr/ontology/FCFR/materializationTemplateInstances> {$subject ?relation ?recordType.} }
WHERE { #4
VALUES (?sType ?relation) {
#( sealit:Ship sealitFR:Ship2Template )
#( sealit:Voyage sealitFR:Voyage2Template )
#( crm:E21_Person sealitFR:Person2Template )
( crm:E40_Legal_Body sealitFR:Legal_Body2Template )
#( crm:E53_Place sealitFR:Place2Template )
##( sealit:Ship_Crew_Employment sealitFR:Ship_Crew_Employment2Template )
#( sealit:Crew_Payment sealitFR:Crew_Payment2Template )
#( sealit:Course sealitFR:Course2Template )
}
$subjectX a ?sType .
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by) $subjectX .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/(sealit:voyages|^sealit:voyage_of) $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Voyage .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/sealit:gave_service_for $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Crew_Payment .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/sealit:had_provided $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Ship_Crew_Employment .}
UNION
{?record crm:P2_has_type ?recordType ; (crm:P67_refers_to|^crm:P67i_is_referred_to_by)/^(crm:P9_consists_of/sealit:had_student) $subjectX . $subjectX a sealit:Course .}
FILTER ( ?recordType != <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/template> )
OPTIONAL { $subjectM owl:sameAs $subjectX . $subjectM crm:P2_has_type <http://www.sealit.gr/DB/type/master>. }
BIND (IF(BOUND($subjectM), $subjectM, $subjectX) AS $subject)
}
